***перейти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перейти.html>перейти́</a> (1433)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-йти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перейти.html>перейти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perejtí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переходить.html>переходи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cross, to get over, to get across</li>
<li>to pass on (to), to proceed (to), to turn (to)</li>
<li>to change, to switch (from/to), to convert (to)</li>
<li>to turn (into), to change, to convert, to transform (to), to go (into)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to exceed, to go beyond (a limit)</li></ol>

***перекат.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекат.html>перека́т</a> (12549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатить.html>перекати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекат.html>перека́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекат.html>перека́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекат.html>перека́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекат.html>перека́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rolling</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">usually in the plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sharp sound, crack <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a shot</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, rumble <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of thunder</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>shoal, shallow, sandbar <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">especially of a river</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***перекатиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекатиться.html>перекати́ться</a> (21862)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатить.html>перекати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатиться.html>перекати́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekatítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатываться.html>перека́тываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roll over</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roll across</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекатывать.html>перека́тывать</a> (30177)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатить.html>перекати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roll <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from one place to another</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатываться.html>перека́тываться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perekátyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатиться.html>перекати́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perekatítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">переката́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekatátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатывать.html>перека́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переката́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roll (all or many things from one place to another)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take (all or many people) for a ride</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to resmooth by rolling (linen, felt, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smooth (all or many items of linen, felt, etc.)</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекатываться.html>перека́тываться</a> (16922)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатывать.html>перека́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekátyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатываться.html>перека́тываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekátyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатиться.html>перекати́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roll over</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roll across</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rumble <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of thunder</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекатывать.html>перека́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekátyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***перекидывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекидывать.html>переки́дывать</a> (22415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">переки́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekíd-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">перекида́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекидывать.html>переки́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekídyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекинуть.html>переки́нуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перекида́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw over, to throw across
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекинуть.html>переки́нуть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perekínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to throw <i>(one after another)</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перекида́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perekidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекидывать.html>переки́дывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekídyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекидываться.html>переки́дываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekídyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекинуться.html>переки́нуться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to leap over</li>
<li>to spread (of a disease)</li>
<li>to throw (one to another)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекидывать.html>переки́дывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekídyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***перекидывающийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекидываться.html>переки́дывающийся</a> (27642)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекидываться.html>переки́дывающийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekídyvajuščijsja</span>)
</p>

***перекинуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекинуться.html>переки́нуться</a> (13148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекинуть.html>переки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекинуться.html>переки́нуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekínutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекидываться.html>переки́дываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to leap over</li>
<li>to spread (of a disease)</li>
<li>to throw (one to another)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекинуть.html>переки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перебро́ситься</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perebrósitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***перекись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекись.html>пе́рекись</a> (20350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о́</a>)кись</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">(ó)kisʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with stress shift of a sort typical for derivatives ending in <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-ь</span>; calque of peroxide.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекись.html>пе́рекись</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pérekisʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекись.html>пе́рекиси</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекись.html>пе́рекиси</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекись.html>пе́рекисей</a></b>)

***перекладывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекладывать.html>перекла́дывать</a> (12329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кла́дывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекладывать.html>перекла́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekládyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переложить.html>переложи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shift, to move, to put/place elsewhere
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекладывать.html>перекла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>но́шу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>другу́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekládyvatʹ</b> nóšu v drugúju rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shift the load to one's other arm</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shift <i>(onto)</i></li>
<li>to interlay <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекладывать.html>перекла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:посуда.html>посу́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:солома.html>соло́мой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekládyvatʹ</b> posúdu solómoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pack crockery between layers of straw</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to set up/put in again
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекладывать.html>перекла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:печка.html>пе́чку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekládyvatʹ</b> péčku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set the stove up again</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to arrange, to transpose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекладывать.html>перекла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:музыка.html>му́зыку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekládyvatʹ</b> na múzyku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set to music</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекладывать.html>перекла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>стихи́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekládyvatʹ</b> v stixí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put into verse</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put too much
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекладывать.html>перекла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:соль.html>со́ли</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хара</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekládyvatʹ</b> sóli (sáxara)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put too much salt (sugar)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trim (sails)</li></ol>

***переключать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переключать.html>переключа́ть</a> (20122)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переключить.html>переключи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переключать.html>переключа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereključátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переключить.html>переключи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to switch, to switch <i>(over to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переключать.html>переключа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ток.html>ток</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereključátʹ</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ток.html>tok</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to switch the current</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переключать.html>переключа́ть</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:телевизионный.html>телевизио́нные</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:канал.html>кана́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereključátʹ</b> (televiziónnyje) kanály</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to switch the (TV) channels</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to switch <i>(over to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переключать.html>переключа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговор.html>разгово́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>другу́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тема.html>те́му</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereključátʹ</b> razgovór na drugúju tému</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to switch/turn the conversation to another subject</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переключать.html>переключа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:производство.html>произво́дство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:велосипед.html>велосипе́дов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereključátʹ</b> zavód na proizvódstvo velosipédov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to switch the factory over to the production of bicycles</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переключать.html>переключа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereključátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переключаться.html>переключа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereključátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переключиться.html>переключи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to switch, to switch over</li>
<li>to switch over <i>(to)</i></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ключи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to switch, to switch <i>(over to)</i>

<li>to switch <i>(over to)</i>
